# Trading Validation Matrix

日期：2026-05-20

执行者：Codex

本文档是 MTP-24 的交易验证矩阵入口，用于把交易语义验证拆成可审计、可自动检查、可回填证据的位置。

本文档不授权执行 Linear issue，不修改 Linear status，不启动 symphony-issue，不创建 Linear Project / Issue，不替代 PR evidence、Linear issue contract 或 Stage Code Audit Report。

## 使用规则

- 每一行的 `Matrix ID` 是稳定锚点，`checks/automation-readiness.sh` 会检查这些锚点是否存在。
- 后续 issue 增加测试、fixtures、read model 或 report evidence 时，必须回填对应矩阵行的 evidence 位置和验证说明。
- 回填证据必须来自本地可重复验证入口，例如 XCTest、fixture、read model snapshot、PR evidence 或 append-only `verification.md` 记录。
- CI 通过、人工观察或 planning notes 不能单独作为交易语义验收证据。
- `bash checks/run.sh` 是统一验证入口；当前 issue 不新增独立 eval 框架。

## 统一边界

- 第一版交易验证只覆盖 Research / Backtest / Paper readiness。
- 标的范围仍为 `BTCUSDT`、`ETHUSDT`、`BNBUSDT`、`SOLUSDT`、`XRPUSDT`。
- 时间粒度仍为 `1m` 和 `5m`。
- Binance 只允许 public read-only market data。
- 禁止 Live trading、signed endpoint、account endpoint、listenKey user data stream、真实 broker action、真实订单提交 / 取消 / 替换、futures leverage / margin action。

## MTP-65 LiveReadiness / LiveBlockedEvidence Read Model Evidence

MTP-65 把 MTP-62 credential endpoint boundary、MTP-63 adapter capability isolation 和 MTP-64 real order lifecycle boundary 聚合成 Core 层最小 read-model-only blocked evidence。`LiveReadiness` 只输出 `blocked` readiness，`LiveBlockedEvidence` 只把 API key、signed endpoint、account endpoint、listenKey user data stream、broker adapter 和 real order lifecycle 映射到已完成 gate / contract anchor，不暴露 adapter、Runtime object、SQLite / DuckDB schema，不提供 command surface，不授权 Live trading。

上游 Gate 1 至 Gate 3 的 Core anchors 仍纳入同一矩阵行：`LiveTradingCredentialEndpointCapability`、`LiveTradingCredentialEndpointFutureGate`、`LiveTradingCredentialEndpointEvidenceKind`、`LiveAdapterIsolationForbiddenCapability`、`LiveAdapterIsolationFutureGate`、`LiveAdapterIsolationEvidenceKind`、`RealOrderLifecycleTerm`、`RealOrderLifecycleFutureGate`、`RealOrderLifecycleForbiddenCapability` 和 `RealOrderLifecycleEvidenceKind`。

上游 Gate 1 至 Gate 3 的 deterministic tests 仍作为 MTP-65 read model 的输入证据：`testLiveTradingCredentialEndpointBoundaryDefinesMTP62GateOneAsFutureOnly`、`testLiveTradingCredentialEndpointBoundaryRejectsSecretSignedAccountAndListenKeyBypass`、`testPublicReadOnlyAdapterCannotUpgradeIntoMTP62CredentialOrAccountCapability`、`testLiveAdapterCapabilityIsolationBoundaryDefinesMTP63GateTwoAsFutureOnly`、`testLiveAdapterCapabilityIsolationBoundaryRejectsExecutionAdapterInstantiationBypass`、`testPublicReadOnlyAdapterCannotInstantiateMTP63LiveAdapterOrExecutionVenueCapability`、`testRealOrderLifecycleBoundaryDefinesMTP64GateThreeAsFutureOnly`、`testRealOrderLifecycleBoundaryRejectsMTP64ForbiddenCapabilityBypass`、`testPaperOrderFillAndPortfolioEvidenceCannotUpgradeToRealOrderLifecycle` 和 `testPublicReadOnlyAdapterCannotUpgradeIntoMTP64RealOrderLifecycleCapability`。

| Evidence location | 验证内容 |
| --- | --- |
| `Sources/Core/LiveTradingBoundary.swift` | `LiveReadinessStatus`、`LiveBlockedCapability`、`LiveBlockedEvidenceKind`、`LiveBlockedEvidence`、`LiveReadiness` 和 deterministic fixture。 |
| `Tests/CoreTests/CoreTests.swift` | `testLiveReadinessDefinesMTP65BlockedReadModelOnlyEvidence`、`testLiveReadinessRejectsMTP65CommandSchemaAndLiveCapabilityBypass` 和 `testLiveBlockedEvidenceKeepsMTP65AllLiveGatesBlocked`。 |
| `docs/contracts/live-trading-boundary-contract.md` | `MTP-65-LIVE-READINESS-BLOCKED-READ-MODEL`、`MTP-65-LIVE-BLOCKED-EVIDENCE-GATES`、`MTP-65-READ-MODEL-ONLY-NON-COMMAND` 和 `MTP-65-SCHEMA-ADAPTER-RUNTIME-NON-EXPOSURE`。 |
| `checks/automation-readiness.sh` | MTP-65 contract / matrix / validation anchors、Core type anchors 和 deterministic test anchors。 |

## MTP-96 / MTP-97 / MTP-98 / MTP-99 / MTP-100 / MTP-101 / MTP-102 issue backfill

MTP-96 issue backfill 保持 `TradingClock` / `PaperRuntimeKernelBoundary` 第一层 boundary evidence。

MTP-97 issue backfill 已回填到 `TVM-PAPER-RUNTIME-KERNEL`，只覆盖 paper-only deterministic routing，不扩大为真实 execution runtime。

MTP-98 issue backfill 已回填到 `TVM-PAPER-RUNTIME-KERNEL`，只覆盖 paper-only pre-trade RiskEngine runtime path，不扩大为 live risk engine、真实账户风控或 broker rejection。

MTP-99 issue backfill 已回填到 `TVM-PAPER-RUNTIME-KERNEL`，只覆盖 paper-only lifecycle coordinator、local order lifecycle transition facts 和 simulated fill 前置状态，不扩大为 OMS、broker router、真实订单状态机、真实 cancel command 或 order-level command UI。

MTP-100 issue backfill 已回填到 `TVM-PAPER-RUNTIME-KERNEL`，只覆盖 paper-only simulated fill / fee / slippage deterministic model、market snapshot、partial / full fill evidence、fixed cost impact、Event Log / Replay fill facts，不扩大为 broker fill、execution report、真实 fee statement、真实成交质量分析、live reconciliation、signed endpoint、account endpoint、broker action 或 real account update。

MTP-101 issue backfill 已回填到 `TVM-PAPER-RUNTIME-KERNEL`，只覆盖 replayed simulated fill -> paper account / portfolio / position / exposure / PnL projection v2 和 App read model consumption，不扩大为真实账户余额、broker position sync、margin、leverage、real PnL、live risk runtime、position command、live command 或交易按钮。

MTP-102 issue backfill 已回填到 `TVM-PAPER-RUNTIME-KERNEL`，只覆盖 Event Log / Replay / Report / Dashboard / Event Timeline evidence chain 和 Stage Code Audit 输入材料，不输出最终 Stage Code Audit Report，不推进下一阶段，不扩大为 OMS、broker router、真实订单、broker fill、execution report、reconciliation、真实账户、Live PRO Console、live command、order form、position command 或交易按钮。

| Issue | Matrix ID | 回填说明 |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `MTP-96` | `TVM-PAPER-RUNTIME-KERNEL` | 已定义 Core 层 `TradingClock` 与 `PaperRuntimeKernelBoundary` deterministic fixture，固定 paper runtime 的时间、session、command intake、event emission、replay 和 module boundary anchors；不实现 live runtime、CommandBus / EventBus / MessageBus、Paper RiskEngine、paper lifecycle coordinator、simulated fill、paper account projection、signed endpoint、account endpoint、listenKey、broker adapter、`LiveExecutionAdapter`、OMS、real order lifecycle、真实 submit / cancel / replace、Live PRO Console、live command 或交易按钮。 |
| `MTP-97` | `TVM-PAPER-RUNTIME-KERNEL` | 已新增 Core 层 `PaperRuntimeCommandBus` / `PaperRuntimeEventBus` / `PaperRuntimeMessageBusRouting` deterministic route，支持 paper session command、paper risk decision、paper lifecycle event 和 simulated fill event 进入既有 `MessageBus` / append-only Event Log；route evidence 保留 source、payload kind、stream、correlation 和 causation，并可从 Event Log / Replay 重建；不实现 live command bus、order-level real command、signed request routing、broker / exchange execution adapter、execution report、broker fill、reconciliation、Paper RiskEngine、paper lifecycle coordinator、paper account projection、Live PRO Console、live command 或交易按钮。 |
| `MTP-98` | `TVM-PAPER-RUNTIME-KERNEL` | 已新增 Core 层 `PaperPreTradeRiskEngineRuntimePath` deterministic path，输入 paper proposal、paper account snapshot、paper exposure 和 paper risk rules，输出 accepted / rejected paper risk decision；rejected decision 通过 MTP-97 routing 写入 `.risk` stream 的 evaluation requested / blocked facts，并可从 Event Log / Replay 重建 route evidence；不实现 live risk engine、真实账户读取、broker position sync、margin、leverage、real pre-trade allow / reject runtime、circuit breaker command、stop trading command、emergency stop、paper lifecycle coordinator、simulated fill / fee / slippage model、paper account projection、Live PRO Console、live command 或交易按钮。 |
| `MTP-99` | `TVM-PAPER-RUNTIME-KERNEL` | 已新增 Core 层 `PaperOrderLocalLifecycleCoordinator` deterministic path，输入 MTP-98 accepted / rejected paper risk decision，输出 proposed、submitted local、accepted local、rejected by paper risk、cancelled local、expired local 和 failed local 的本地 lifecycle transition fact；accepted local 只作为 `PaperOrderSimulatedFillPrecondition`，每个 transition 通过 MTP-97 routing 写入 `.paper` stream 并可从 Event Log / Replay 重建 route evidence；不实现 OMS、broker router、真实 order lifecycle、真实 submit / cancel / replace、execution report、broker fill、reconciliation、单笔 order cancel button、order-level command UI、Live PRO Console、live command 或交易按钮。 |
| `MTP-100` | `TVM-PAPER-RUNTIME-KERNEL` | 已新增 Core 层 `PaperSimulatedFillMarketSnapshot`、`PaperSimulatedFillCompletion`、`PaperSimulatedFillPriceSource`、`PaperSimulatedFillEventLogBoundary`、`PaperSimulatedFillPublication`、`PaperSimulatedFillReplayPath` 和 MTP-100 deterministic fixtures；simulated fill 输入绑定 MTP-99 accepted-local precondition、market snapshot、allowed paper order intent 和 deterministic fill assumption；full / partial evidence 分别固定 remaining quantity、fee assumption、slippage assumption、fill price assumption 和 cost impact；fill evidence 通过 MTP-97 routing 写入 `.paper` stream 并可 replay；不实现 broker fill、execution report parser、真实 fee statement、真实成交质量分析、live reconciliation、signed endpoint、account endpoint、broker action、real account update、Live PRO Console、live command、order form 或交易按钮。 |
| `MTP-101` | `TVM-PAPER-RUNTIME-KERNEL` | 已新增 Core 层 `PaperAccountProjectionSnapshot`、`PaperPositionProjectionSnapshot`、`PaperPortfolioPnLSummary`、`PaperAccountPortfolioProjectionV2Snapshot`、`PaperAccountPortfolioProjectionV2Path` 和 MTP-101 deterministic fixture；projection 输入只能来自 replayed `.paper.simulatedFillRecorded` facts，输出 account cash / available paper balance / equity、position quantity / average entry / market value、exposure 和 paper PnL summary，并通过 Persistence / App read model 被 Report / Dashboard / Risk / Portfolio 消费；不实现真实账户余额读取、broker position sync、margin、leverage、real PnL、live risk runtime、signed endpoint、account endpoint、broker action、position command、live command 或交易按钮。 |

## MTP-89 issue backfill

MTP-90 issue backfill 保留为既有 readiness anchor；MTP-90 / MTP-91 issue backfill 已追加到同一 `TVM-LIVE-AUDIT-INCIDENT-STOP` 矩阵入口，保持 audit trail gates 和 incident replay gates 仍是 Future / forbidden contract。MTP-92 issue backfill 继续追加到同一矩阵入口，保持 stop / shutdown / restore gates 仍是 Future / forbidden contract。MTP-93 issue backfill 继续追加到同一矩阵入口，保持 blocked evidence isolation 仍是 read-model-only / paper-only boundary，不升级为 command 或 runtime。MTP-94 issue backfill 继续追加到同一矩阵入口，只把 audit trail、incident replay、emergency stop、shutdown 和 restore 的 blocked reasons 接入 Report / Dashboard / Event Timeline 只读展示面。
